<p><b>Alexander Leroy Hubbard</b> (born May 23, 1993), better known by his =
stage name <b>Fantasy A</b>, is an American rapper from <a href=3D"https://=
en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Seattle" title=3D"Seattle">Seattle</a>, Washington wo=
rking in the <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hip_hop_music" title=
=3D"Hip hop music">hip hop</a> genre, as well as a songwriter, actor, and a=
uthor. He is best known for his extensive guerrilla marketing and performan=
ce in the film <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=3DFant=
asy_A_Gets_a_Mattress&amp;action=3Dedit&amp;redlink=3D1" class=3D"new" titl=
e=3D"Fantasy A Gets a Mattress (page does not exist)">Fantasy A Gets a Matt=
ress</a>.
</p>
<meta property=3D"mw:PageProp/toc">
<h2><span class=3D"mw-headline" id=3D"Early_life">Early life</span><span cl=
ass=3D"mw-editsection"><span class=3D"mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a hr=
ef=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=3DFantasy_A&amp;action=3De=
dit&amp;section=3D1&amp;editintro=3DTemplate:BLP_editintro" title=3D"Edit s=
ection: Early life">edit</a><span class=3D"mw-editsection-bracket">]</span>=
</span></h2>
<p>Fantasy A was born in <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Seattle" =
title=3D"Seattle">Seattle</a>, Washington, where he was diagnosed with auti=
sm at the age of three<sup id=3D"cite_ref-1" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D=
"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fantasy_A#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup>. He att=
ended <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=3DThurgood_Mars=
hall_Elementary&amp;action=3Dedit&amp;redlink=3D1" class=3D"new" title=3D"T=
hurgood Marshall Elementary (page does not exist)">Thurgood Marshall Elemen=
tary</a> as well as <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cleveland_High=
_School_(Seattle)" title=3D"Cleveland High School (Seattle)">Cleveland High=
 School (Seattle)</a> before graduating from <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedi=
a.org/wiki/The_Center_School_(Seattle,_Washington)" class=3D"mw-redirect" t=
itle=3D"The Center School (Seattle, Washington)">The Center School (Seattle=
, Washington)</a> in 2011. While in high school he gained an interest in li=
terature and wrote three books later published as <i>School Rich</i> (2012)=
, <i>Life in the Eyes of an Autistic Person</i> (2012), and <i>Life in the =
World of Gabe Fabens and Sage the Scholar</i> (2013).
</p>
<h2><span class=3D"mw-headline" id=3D"Career">Career</span><span class=3D"m=
w-editsection"><span class=3D"mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href=3D"ht=
tps://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=3DFantasy_A&amp;action=3Dedit&amp;=
section=3D2&amp;editintro=3DTemplate:BLP_editintro" title=3D"Edit section: =
Career">edit</a><span class=3D"mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the mid-2010s Fantasy A began to gain notice in the Seattle area for =
his guerrilla promotional campaigns where he would cover every neighborhood=
 in posters for his books and music. The campaigns were so extensive that i=
t was covered by both <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Stranger=
_(newspaper)" title=3D"The Stranger (newspaper)">The Stranger (newspaper)</=
a> and the <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Seattle_Weekly" title=
=3D"Seattle Weekly">Seattle Weekly</a>.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-Seattle_Weekly_2=
-0" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fantasy_A#=
cite_note-Seattle_Weekly-2">[2]</a></sup><sup id=3D"cite_ref-The_Stranger_(=
newspaper)_3-0" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wik=
i/Fantasy_A#cite_note-The_Stranger_(newspaper)-3">[3]</a></sup><sup id=3D"c=
ite_ref-South_Seattle_Emerald_4-0" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://e=
n.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fantasy_A#cite_note-South_Seattle_Emerald-4">[4]</a></=
sup>
</p><p>In 2017 Fantasy A starred in the short film Fantasy A Gets Jacked wh=
ich started his interest in film.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-KNKX-FM_5-0" class=3D"=
reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fantasy_A#cite_note-KNK=
X-FM-5">[5]</a></sup> In 2019 he became a reoccurring guest on KJR-FM's The=
 Wake Up Show where he reviewed movies.
</p><p>In 2023 Fantasy A starred in the feature film Fantasy A Gets a Mattr=
ess, which gained a cult following, winning Best Narrative Feature at the S=
eattle Black Film Festival before going on to sold-out runs<sup id=3D"cite_=
ref-6" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fantasy=
_A#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup><sup id=3D"cite_ref-In_Their_Own_League_7-0" c=
lass=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fantasy_A#cite_=
note-In_Their_Own_League-7">[7]</a></sup><sup id=3D"cite_ref-KUOW-FM_8-0" c=
lass=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fantasy_A#cite_=
note-KUOW-FM-8">[8]</a></sup> at <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/N=
orthwest_Folklife_Festival" class=3D"mw-redirect" title=3D"Northwest Folkli=
fe Festival">Northwest Folklife Festival</a>, The Beacon Cinema, the <a hre=
f=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grand_Illusion_Cinema" title=3D"Grand Il=
lusion Cinema">Grand Illusion Cinema</a>, and opening the Northwest Film Fo=
rum's Local Sightings Film Festival.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-KUOW_9-0" class=3D"=
reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fantasy_A#cite_note-KUO=
W-9">[9]</a></sup><sup id=3D"cite_ref-Seattle_Times_10-0" class=3D"referenc=
e"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fantasy_A#cite_note-Seattle_Tim=
es-10">[10]</a></sup><sup id=3D"cite_ref-My_Ballard_11-0" class=3D"referenc=
e"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fantasy_A#cite_note-My_Ballard-=
11">[11]</a></sup><sup id=3D"cite_ref-Runta_Somali_News_Magazine_12-0" clas=
s=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fantasy_A#cite_not=
e-Runta_Somali_News_Magazine-12">[12]</a></sup>
</p>
